%% \Ram: anantena sahaitaani iti puurva.m hi anantaaya iti anantasya vide"samadhyapuujyatayaa padamuktam| atra tvaasanatvena padaantaramityavirodha.h||
%% This last verse states that dharma, j~naana, vairaagya and ai"svarya
%% have respectively the mantras vyomin vyomin, vyaapin vyaapin, 
%% aruupin aruupin, and prathama prathama.  The mantras tejasteja.h and jyotirjyoti.h
%% therefore belong respectively to the Kar.nikaa and to Ananta,
%% for whom, for \Ram, a different mantra is assigned when he is among the other
%% Vidye"sas.  But could it be that he has another mantra because he is another Ananta?
% dvaatri.m"satkesaramantraa.h

%% consonants (excluding ha and k.sa): 5 principal vargas (25) + semivowels (4) + sibilants (3).
%% It is the var.nas with which the kesaras are associated in the Kir.

%% It is clear here that this is not the Vidye"svara Ananta, but rather
%% the supporter of the brahmaa.n.da at the very bottom: not only is the other
%% Ananta about to be placed later, but in \Mat\KP\ 1:82c--87 separate mantras
%% were identified as belonging to the Ananta-as-throne.  This bottom
%% Ananta is sometimes called Huuhuka (\Svacch\ 10:?? and 11:22--24,
%% where it is explained that he resides only in his own "Sakti and is therefore called
%% anaa"srita [is this perhaps an explanation of the 3 contiguous epithets in
%% the Vyomavyaapimantra `anantaaya anaathaaya anaa"sritaaya' which
%% in \Mat\KP\ 1 are assigned to the 1st 3 vidye"svara??]);
%% but elsewhere Ananta and Huuhuka are distinguished (e.g. SP3, III:80--83).

ayamatraanu.s.thaanakrama.h---"si.sya.m "sa"nkhavaaditrani.hsvanai.h [vividhairmaa"ngalyai.h] snaata.m candanaa[di]bhi.h vilepita.m praav.rta"svetavastra.m saaradaarumaye pii.the nive"sya, duurvaadima"ngalai.h asak.rd nirmarcya sarvamantrai.h "sikhaabhedenaabhimantrya, yaagabhuumerbahi.h uttarasyaa.m di"si dvihastocchritasu"svetakamalamadhyasthapii.the dhvajatora.napataakaadyupa"sobhite .a.s.taabhirvidye"svarajaptai.h kala"sai.h krame.na puurvaabhimukhamuttaraabhimukho guru.h vyomavyaapinamuccaarayan abhi.secayet| tata.h praav.rtaanaardra"suklavaaso .antara.m bhuu.sa.nai.h bhuu.sayet iti||

\Ram
k.rtapuurva"sivatanurapyasaavatyuccapii.thastho .abhi.sekajalenopahataja"nghaadiriti tacchaucapuurva.m puna.h "sivatanu.m k.rtvaa, ma.n.dalastha.m bhagavanta.m pra.namya, prabhutvacihna.m pii.tho.s.nii.sacchatrapaaduka.m tasya samarpayet| "sivaj~naana.m ca pustakaatmakameva| tatasta.m parame"svarapaadayorvinipaatya, `gurutve aya.m mayaa tava aaj~nayaa niyukta.h' iti parame"svara.m vij~naapya, atha anantara.m so .api "si.sya.h eva.m vaktavya.h bhavet| yathaa---`putraka yo .aya.m matta.h sakaa"saat praapta.h adhikaara.h, sa tvayi sthita iti k.rtvaa "sivaaj~nayaa "saastravihitena krame.na paalya.h, na tu lobhaadinaa' iti| tato .agnau mantraan tarpayet ityaacaaryasyaabhi.seka.h||

\chapter
% samudaayaprakara.nam Chapter 15
% [ai"svaratejomahimaa]
atha sa.mk.sepato vak.sye vidhaanamidamuttamam|
yena vij~naatamaatre.na phala.m praapnotyabhiipsitam|| 15:1||
tejo yatsarvaga.m suuk.sma.m pu.mviiryaatmanyavasthitam|
tadeva sarvadevaanaa.m mantraa.naa.m ca mahaatmanaam|| 15:2||
yenaadhi.s.thitasaamarthyaadindriyaa.ni svake svake|
pravartante .arthasantaane; yadaj~naanopab.r.mhitam|| 15:3||
yathepsitaphalaavaaptyai na kadaacitprasajyate|
tadviiryamai"svara.m vedya.m yattantramakhila.m jagat|| 15:4||
pravartate; munivyaaghra sa evaaha.m yadaa mati.h|
ni.hsandigdhatayaa vacmi japata.h sampravartate|| 15:5||
na tadasti tadaa tasya trailokye .apyaprasaadhitam| % [mantrasaadhane .sa.nmaargaa.h]
japo rak.saa parij~naana.m ni"scaya.h sattvameva ca|| 15:6||
vrataani cetyaya.m maargo vidhe.h .so.dhaa vyavasthita.h| % [asiddhasya mantrasya siddhiikara.nopaaya.h]
yadaa mantrii vratopaattaviirye.naatiiva bhuuri.naa|| 15:7||
b.r.mhita.h sahasaa mantrastatasta.m prati "sa"nkita.h|
na "saknoti bala.m tasya so.dhu.m svalpavapurmanu.h|| 15:8||
kalpoktamakhila.m caasya yathaavatparivistaraat|
nirvartita.m kimadyaapi na mantro .asminva"saanuga.h|| 15:9||
na ca pa"syaami vighnaanaa.m svalpamapyatra ce.s.titam|
utk.r.s.tavapu.saatmaana.m sotsaahamajugupsitam|| 15:10||
tadaa vibhu.m "siva.m dhyaatvaa kar.nikaayaa.m "subhojjvalam|
praa.naayaamena sa.mti.s.thet tacca mantramanusmaran|| 15:11||
smara.naattasya tattejoviirye.naatibaliiyasaa|
pa"syetparaa"nmukha.m mantra.m pramlaanavadana.m mune|| 15:12||
tadaa tena prakartavyo vidhire.sa nivartaka.h|
jyotirjyoti.hpada.m madhye saadhyavar.navidarbhitam|| 15:13||
